def speak(text):
    if text == "welcome":
        playsound("assets/welcome_melah_thai.wav")
    else:
        # fallback: use TTS
        speaker.say(text)
        speaker.runAndWait()

import os
import time

def cleanup_old_audio(folder, expire_seconds=86400):  # 1 ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô
    now = time.time()
    for f in os.listdir(folder):
        fpath = os.path.join(folder, f)
        if os.path.isfile(fpath) and now - os.path.getmtime(fpath) > expire_seconds:
            os.remove(fpath)

import os
from gtts import gTTS
from playsound import playsound

def cleanspeak(text, lang='th'):
    tts = gTTS(text=text, lang=lang)
    filename = "temp_speak.wav"
    tts.save(filename)
    playsound(filename)
    os.remove(filename)  # üî• ‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏û‡∏π‡∏î

def cleanspeak(text):
    tts = gTTS(text=text, lang='th')
    filename = "temp_speak.wav"
    tts.save(filename)
    playsound(filename)
    os.remove(filename)

def speak_direct(text):
    engine = pyttsx3.init()
    engine.setProperty('voice', 'Pattara')  # ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Zira
    engine.say(text)
    engine.runAndWait()

üì¶ ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ:
def load_summaries(folder, date=None):
    summaries = []
    for file in os.listdir(folder):
        if file.endswith(".txt") and (date in file if date else True):
            with open(os.path.join(folder, file), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                summaries.append(f.read())
    return "\n---\n".join(summaries)

def load_memory_month(month: str, year: str = "2025"):
    folder = f"Melah_Memory_Summary/{year}/{month}/"
    memory = []
    for file in os.listdir(folder):
        with open(os.path.join(folder, file), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            memory.append(f.read())
    return "\n---\n".join(memory)
